										 FROM TaxProgramTable tpt

										 LEFT JOIN InstitutionTable inst ON inst.ID = inb.InstitutionID

										 LEFT JOIN InstitutionBudgetTable inb ON inb.ID = tpt.InstitutionBudgetID

										 UNION ALL

										 LEFT JOIN InstitutionTable inst ON inst.ID = inb.InstitutionID
